style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On September 27, 2023, the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of GameStop Corp. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;), with Ryan Cohen abstaining, unanimously appointed Mr. Cohen, as the President, Chief Executive Officer and Chairman effective immediately. Mr. Cohen is currently the Executive Chairman but will relinquish such title upon appointment as Chairman.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">In satisfaction of the disclosure required by Regulation S-K Items 401(b), (d) and (e), the information contained in the Company&#8217;s Proxy Statement, filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on May 2, 2023, is incorporated by reference herein. No family relationships exist between Mr. Cohen and any of the Company&#8217;s other directors or other executive officers. There are no other arrangements between Mr. Cohen and any other person pursuant to which he was selected as an officer, nor are there any transactions to which the Company is or was a participant and in which Mr. Cohen has a material interest subject to disclosure under Item 404(a) of Regulation S-K.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">In connection with his appointment, Mr. Cohen will assume the role of principal executive officer from Mark H. Robinson effective immediately and his responsibilities will include the oversight of all other executive officers, including Mr. Robinson. Mr. Robinson will remain the Company&#8217;s General Counsel and Secretary, with responsibilities including administrative matters, corporate development, and legal affairs.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Mr. Cohen will not receive any compensation for serving as the Company&#8217;s President, Chief Executive Officer and Chairman. He will continue to engage in various business activities and pursuits outside of the Company.</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New
